Test NMSE           : 6.43e-06

============================================================
GT Equivalence Verification (PO39)
============================================================
GT: F0*sin(t) - alpha*v**c0 - beta*exp(-Abs(x))*v - mu*(c1 - v**c2)*v
Candidate formulas: 50

GT (fixed) simplifies to a sum of four distinct parts:
- time-only sinusoid: \(0.3852302349\sin(t)\)
- cubic in \(v\): \(-0.0589613102064644\,v^3\)
- linear-in-\(v\) times \(e^{-|x|}\): \(-0.111443697234506\, v\,e^{-|x|}\)
- linear and cubic from \(-\mu(1-v^2)v\): \(-0.332588418365738\,v + 0.332588418365738\,v^3\)

So overall:
\[
GT = 0.38523\sin(t)\;-\;0.11144\,v e^{-|x|}\;-\;0.33259\,v\;+\;(0.33259-0.05896)\,v^3
\]
i.e. it depends on:
- \(\sin(t)\) (pure \(t\))
- \(v e^{-|x|}\) (coupled \(x,v\) via \(|x|\))
- \(v\) and \(v^3\)
and **has no** plain polynomials in \(x\), no \(x^2,x^3\) terms, no \(e^{kx}\) without \(|x|\), etc.

Key structural requirement for any match (even conditionally on a plausible domain like \(x\ge 0\) or \(x\le 0\)):
- must be able to produce a \(\sin(t)\) term (or a cosine with phase shift),
- must be able to produce a \(v e^{-|x|}\) term (conditionally \(e^{-|x|}=e^{-x}\) if \(x\ge 0\), or \(e^{x}\) if \(x\le 0\)),
- must be able to produce both \(v\) and \(v^3\) with independent coefficients (or at least the correct combined coefficients),
- and must avoid extra unavoidable terms in \(x\), \(t\), or mixed forms.

Now check candidates.

1. Has only \(x\)-polynomials, \(e^{c2 x}\), \(v\), \(v^3\), and \(x^{c5}e^{c6 t}\). No \(\sin(t)\) unless you force weird \(x^{c5}e^{c6 t}\) to become \(\sin(t)\) (impossible). Also no \(v e^{-|x|}\) coupling. **No.**

2. Has \(v\), \(v|v|\) (i.e. \(v^2\operatorname{sign}(v)\)), and \(e^{c7 t}\cos(c8 t)\). You can get a sinusoid in \(t\) only if \(c7=0\), then cosine can phase-shift to sine. But there is still no \(v e^{-|x|}\) term, and it has polynomial-in-\(x\) terms \(x^3,x^2,x\) unless set to 0 (possible). Still missing \(v e^{-|x|}\). **No.**

3. Has \(e^{c2 x}\) and \(v^3,v,vx\). No sinusoid in \(t\) (only \(x^{c4}e^{c5 t}\), not sinusoidal), and no \(v e^{-|x|}\). **No.**

4. Has \(v^3\) and \(v\) but no \(\sin(t)\) and no \(v e^{-|x|}\). **No.**

5. Has \(e^{c2 x}\), \(v^3\), \(v\), and \(exp(c4*sin(...))\). That last term is \(e^{(\text{sin})}\), not a linear sine; cannot equal \(A\sin(t)\) for all \(t\) on any interval unless coefficient is 0 (then it disappears). If you set it to 0 you lose the needed \(\sin(t)\). Also no \(v e^{-|x|}\). **No.**

6. Same issue as 5, and no \(v e^{-|x|}\). **No.**

7. Same as 5 plus \(x^3\). Still cannot produce linear \(\sin(t)\) and lacks \(v e^{-|x|}\). **No.**

8. Has \(tanh(\cdot)\) in \(x\), \(v^3\), \(v e^{c5 t}\) (time exponential, not \(e^{-|x|}\)), \(v\), and \(x^{c8}e^{c9 t}\). No pure \(\sin(t)\) term, and no \(v e^{-|x|}\). **No.**

9. Has \(e^{c1 x}\), \(v x^2\), constants, \(v\), \(e^{c7 t}\), \(v^3\). No sinusoid; no \(v e^{-|x|}\) (only \(e^{c1 x}\) without \(v\) multiplying). Could try to make \(v x^2\) mimic \(v e^{-|x|}\) (impossible). **No.**

10. Similar to 1: no sinusoid, no \(v e^{-|x|}\). **No.**

11. Has \(exp(c4*sin(...))\) and \(v|v|\). Still no linear \(\sin(t)\) term (unless you kill the exp(sin) term, then none), and no \(v e^{-|x|}\). **No.**

12. Has \(e^{c1 x}\), \(v^3\), \(v\), \(v x^2\), constant, \(e^{c9 t}\). No sinusoid; no \(v e^{-|x|}\). **No.**

13. Has \(v|v|\) and \(e^{c1 x}\), \(e^{c7 t}\). No sinusoid; no \(v e^{-|x|}\). **No.**

14. Has \(exp(c4*sin(...))\) and \(v^3\) and \(v x^2\). No linear \(\sin(t)\), no \(v e^{-|x|}\). **No.**

15. Has cosine in \(t\) (good: can phase shift to sine), and has \(v^3\) and \(v\). But it has **no** \(v e^{-|x|}\) term at all. Also has polynomial \(x\) terms that can be zeroed, but missing the crucial \(x\)-dependent damping term. **No.**

16. Has \(\sin(c5 e^{c6 t}+c7 x+c8)\) (mixed \(x,t\) inside sine), not separable as \(\sin(t)\) unless you do impossible constraints (e.g., remove \(x\) dependence by setting \(c7=0\), but still \(\sin(c5 e^{c6 t}+c8)\) is not \(\sin(t)\) for all \(t\)). Also no \(v e^{-|x|}\). **No.**

17. Polynomial in \(x\), \(v x^2\), \(v\), and \(x^{c8}e^{c9 t}\). No sinusoid; no \(v e^{-|x|}\). **No.**

GT: F0*sin(t) - alpha*v**c0 - beta*exp(-Abs(x))*v - mu*(c1 - v**c2)*v

I need to analyze each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `-0.0589613*v³ - 0.332588*v*(1 - v²) - 0.111444*v*exp(-|x|) + 0.385230*sin(t)`

Since x > 0 on this domain, |x| = x, so:
**GT = -0.0589613*v³ - 0.332588*v + 0.332588*v³ - 0.111444*v*exp(-x) + 0.385230*sin(t)**
**GT = 0.273627*v³ - 0.332588*v - 0.111444*v*exp(-x) + 0.385230*sin(t)**

Wait, let me recalculate:
- `-0.332588*v*(1-v²) = -0.332588*v + 0.332588*v³`
- Combined v³: `-0.0589613 + 0.332588 = 0.273627`v³

So GT = **0.273627*v³ - 0.332588*v - 0.111444*v*exp(-x) + 0.385230*sin(t)**

The GT has these basis functions:
1. v³
2. v
3. v*exp(-x)
4. sin(t)

Now I'll check each candidate for the ability to reproduce these exact basis functions.

- exp(c2*x) with c2<0 gives exp(-x) but multiplied by constant, not by v → needs v*exp(-x), not exp(-x) alone ✗
- x^c5*exp(c6*t) ≠ sin(t) ✗
- Missing v*exp(-x) and sin(t)

- Actually, we need the x-polynomial terms to be 0 (set c0=c1=c2=c3=0), and we need v³ but only have v*|v|.
